1b1(kha): g.yung drung lha yi skad du na/
2a1(kha): sad la drung mu mu ye/ ha ra du par shag sal le sal/ gyer spungs sad la gu dun
2a2(kha): h+run/ gyer zhi tan tra spungs la e ma ho/ gang zag mi yi skad du na/ bskal srid grangs
2a3(kha): med byung ba ste/ bder gshegs bskal pa'i grangs rtsis la/ lha gshen srid pa thams cad kyi
2b1(kha): 'gro ba'i don ni rab mdzad pa/ khyad par ngo mtshar dpag pa'i mdo/ 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus cig na/ yi mkhyen thugs rje bdal pa'i dbyings/ stong pa mu med klong nyid nas/ 
2b2(kha): gsal ba'i ye shes dbyings su khyab/ thugs jo' a dang rang bzhan las/ ngobo nyid kyi glong na zni/ de las gsal ba'i rang bzhin byung / gsal ba'i ngo bor 'di stong bhar/ 'de lnga'i rang
2b3(kha): bzhin sku lnga'i dbyings/ sku lnga'i ngo bo ye shes lnga/ rigs lnga rgyal ba'i zhing du grub/ rang bzhin lhun grub mi 'gyur gnas/ sku gsum ngo bo 'du 'bral med/ thugs rje tshad med 
2b4(kha): bzhi dang ldan/ yi shes lnga y dbyings nas dgongs/ 'gag med thugs rjze'i sprul pa las/ lha gzhin srid pa dpag med 'byung / lha gzhen srid pa dpag med kyis/ 'gro ba'i don ni 
2b5(kha): dpag med 'gyed/ ma rig las dang snang 'khrul las/ khams gsum rgyu drug bar ma do/ gnas pa'i sems can zhen chags 'khor/ mrig las dang skye 'phel las/ grangs med 
2b6(kha): mi mthun gzugs su grub/ rigs drug lam lnga'i skye sgo dad/ khams gsum 'khor ba'i skye gnas brgyud/ ma rig dug lnga'i gzhen bskul byas/ zhen cing chags pa 'khor 
3a1(kha): y/ ba'i rgyu/ las kyi rnam rmin dug lnga bsags/ 'bras bya ngan song rgyu drug smin/ bskal srid tig mtha' med par 'khor/ rten gnas 'byung ba lnga ru grub/ rnam shes 
3a2(kha): lus sems rten 'brel la/ skye rgas na 'che las dbang 'byung / ma rig 'khrul pa'i las dbang gis/ sdug bsngal dpag med sbyong bar 'byung / gzugs med gzugs khams 'dod 
3a3(kha): khams dang / zhe sdang 'dod chags gti mug dang / phrag dogng rgyal le lo dang / pham ltung sdug bsngal dpag med la/ skye bzhi las kyis sbyong ba rnams/ lha gzhen srid pa'i thugs 
3a4(kha): rje yis/ thar par 'dren zhing bde bar 'khod/ thugs rjes 'dul ba bon gyis ni/ ma rig 'khor ba'i bdud bcom nas/ 'bras bu s+dzogs sangs rgyas pa yang / lha gnhen srid pa'i 
3a5(kha): thugs rdje'// bskal srid grangs med 'byung ba ste/ sems can las kyang bsam las 'das/ de dag thar par drang ba'i phyir/ lha gnhen srid pa thams cad ni/ rim gyis 'byon zhing 
3a6(kha): 'gro don mdzad/ bskal srid thog mtha' bskal grangs bzhin/ bder gshegs sprul pa'i rnam grangs kyis/ 'gro ba'i don ni rgyas par mdzad/ de ltar 'dul ba'i zhing du srid/ de yi 
3b1(kha): dus dang de'i tche na/ 'og men s+dzogs sku'i zhing khams su / ye shes lnga yi thugs rje dang / lha gnhen srid pa'i sprul pa las/ 'gro don dpag med mdzad pa yi/ gshen rab stong dang 
3b2(kha): rtsa gnyis kyis/ shes rab blo rtsal sbyangs pa'i mchog/ 'bum khri glog gi lce can la/ bskal srid grangs med bon rtcsis ni/ 'gro don dpag med mdzad pa'i phyir/ rab gsal / 
3b3(kha): mu tsho ldam drug gis/ me tog pad ma stong ldan ni/ slob dpon gnen la phrul nas kyang / gus phyag 'tshal nas zhus pa'i mod/ kyi slob dpon gnhen rab chen po lags/ hi 
3b4(kha): ltar srid cing gnas pa yi/ spyi yi bskal pa ci ltar lags/ yas mar tshad ni ci bzhin lags/ lha gnhen srid pa ci ltar 'byon/ 'byon pa'i gnas ni gang du mchis/ 'dul 
3b5(kha): ba'i gnas ni ci ltar gnas/ mi tsho' tshad ni ci tsam mchis/ gshen rab sku tsho' tshad ci ltar/ 'dul ngag con sde bka' rgyud dang / bstan pa'i yun ni ci ltar gnas/ 'gro 
3b6(kha): ba'i don ni ci lthar s+dzogs/ sku gzugs gsung rab thams cad dang / sku gdung mchod rten thams cad ni/ gang du rgyas par 'byung ba dang / 'gro don s+dzogs nas gang du gnas/ chags 
4a1(kha): / nas na rid znid brcyudang / re se rgyal por rbani/ rtag par gn am 'jig gas nting / 'jig na tci ltar 'jog p adang / teng na ga u nying pani/ gsheon rob/ 
4a2(kha): chen pos bshad du gsol/ de ltar mu chos zhus pa dang / 'bum khri glog gi tha can gyis/ mu tsho nyid la bka' stsal pa/ de ltar zhus pa rab tu legs/ lha gzhen sred pa / 
4a3(kha): thams cad ni/ ye khyab dbyings kyi ngo bo las/ thabs shes sprul pa'i dbyings las ni/ ye 'byung lha ghen sred pa gsum/ lha ghen srid pa de gsum gyi/ nga dang thugs rje'i sprul pa 
4a4(kha): las/ lha gnhen srid pa thams cad 'byung / ston pas 'dul ba'i bon du sred/ srid chags snang sred gnas pa na/ lha gzhen srid pa bon gyis ni/ thar par yongs su 'dren pa'o// spyi 
4a5(kha): yi bskal pa chen po gsum/ sgos kyi bskal pa dpag tu med/ bskal phran 'jig stong du ma 'ong / yas mar tshad ni rang thung la/ lha gzhen srid pa rim gyis 'byung / 'byon 
4a6(kha): gnas stong gsum spyi phud kyi/ rang 'byung chen po byin ldan gnas/ lhun ldan 'ol mo lung ring gi/ gnas mchog stong dang rtsa gnyis su / gshen rab stong dang rtsa gnyis ni/ yab 
4b1(kha): dang yum la sku brten cing / gnas mchog de ru 'byin nas kyang / 'gro ba'i don ni ram gyis mdzad/ thams cad thar par dbyings su 'dren/ 'dul ba'i zhing ni khams gsum dang / 
4b2(kha): snang sed rab 'byams zhing khams so// me cho rang pthung 'phel 'grib 'byung / gnhen rab sku tsho de bzhin no// 'drul ngag bden pa bon sde bka' rgyud kyang / bstan pa yun bzhin 
4b3(kha): rgyas par rab gnas shing / sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don mthar byin nas/ 'gro don 'dul ba'i tshad ni s+dzogs pa'o// sku gzugs gsung rab sku gdung mchod rten yang / 'gro don 
4b4(kha): s+dzogs pa bzhin du s+dzogs shing yal/ re yi rgyal po re rab kyang / nga dang ngo bo mnyam par gcig/ 'gro don mthar pbyin s+dzogs pa dang / chags gnas snang sred snod bcud kyang / 
4b5(kha): chags zhing gnas pa 'jig cing stong / chags gnas 'jig stong tshad du mnyam/ stong pa bon nyid dbyings kyi shlong / de yi bar du gnas pa ni/ yar gyi ya thog dpag med ni/ mar 
4b6(kha): gyi ma thog ring mo dang / bar gyi khug chen zhug chung la/ bun thang bun thang 'gyur du gnas/ yas mar gnyis ni dpag tu med/ gnhen rab rabs bdun 'gro don ni/ bar gyi 
5a1(kha): bskal pa zhugs chungo// stong dang rtsa gnyis 'gro don ni/ bar gyi bskal pa zhugs chen no// stong dang rtsa gnyis s+dzogs pa dang / de ni bskal pa chen po gcig/ lha / 
5a2(kha): gzhin sred pa thams cad ni/ ram gyis 'gro ba'i don la 'byon/ 'gro ba'i don ni dpag med la/ stong pa tsam gyis bde bar 'dren/ stong dang rtsa gnyis 'byon gnas ni/ stong gsum 
5a3(kha): stong gi pyi pud de/ bde bar gshegs pa'i byin brlabs pa/ khyad par 'phags pa'i gnas mchog nyid/ rin chen 'od grub chen po ste/ 'ol mo lung rang bya ba ru/ yab dang yum la 
5a4(kha): / sku brten nas/ 'gro ba'i don la 'byon pa'o// de yi dus dang de' che na/ bskal pa snga ma do ni stongs/ sems can grangs med bsam 'das kyang / 'khor ba'i las la thar pa thob
5a5(kha): sdug bsngal las thar 'dir slabs so// bskal pa chen po de stongs nas/ phyi ma'i bskal pa rim gyis chags/ bskal pa de yi dus nyid na/ rgyu 'byung lnga la brten pa yi/ snang srid 
5a6(kha): rab 'byams zhing khams ni/ dpag tu med pa srid cing chags/ rgyu rkyen rten 'brel lnga brten pa'i/ sems can mi mthun dpag med pa/ bsam las 'das kyis ryen gnas / 
5b1(kha): o/ bstals bhom dpag to/ rdpa bab d'od / bstan pans 'dana / bstan gan 'db gon cas zhote gd nyi shoyi slo kyo/ 'rob bo/ 
5b2(kha): ble gi l ryog n/ bye ba'i gna la bya 'lag pa'igna mtshig lab lu '/ bd ba gzeg pa 'kbyen pa'i gnas / byen bshar bhin bun grub a'i
5b3(kha): din cen d 'b gan nyi du/ b ghoned pacas khadang / gzen rab tyi da rtsa gd zha/ rang grub cen po gan mtshog te/ bya par lag lpala'ig 'i
5b4(kha): gna mtshag nyi dang rtsa gnyis du/ ran 'bya cen po'i rten tshog tgsu du 'bar la'og te/ btshod dan nyi da rtsa gnyis tsar/ 'gro bdon 'thags dgs
5b5(kha): nasphadg dum la gu brten pa/ seMsi lung l gyu dul ni / 'gro bcad pa 'dan pa'// el shye gi gn ban te/ kar kyi lung 'ag sbra ste s/ bhra b stan 
5b6(kha): n dod las stye/ ba lang spyod ni rni las stye/ 'dam blang mzhi mala nas sy/ skye ba gnas bzo' m regs kyi/ chi y tchad kyang rang blag la/ lus kyi thad kyang chi byu ste/ shar 
6a1(kha): e/ lus 'phags po'i lus cad ni/ gu thad dum thu s gnyis so// tshe tshad brgya phrag bcu ru gnas/ byang gi shra ma snyan gyi lus/ tshad ni gu tshad bcu drug go/ che / 
6a2(kha): tshad brgya brag lnga ru gnas/ thub kyi ba lang kpyod kyi lus/ tshad n gu tshad brgyad yod d// che ye tshad ni brgya prag gnyis/ bcu phrag lnga ru gnas pa yin/ lho ye 'dzam bu 
6a3(kha): gling gi mi/ lus kyi tshad ni khru bzhi'// spyir na tshe tshad bcu phrag bcu/ rang thung 'phel 'greb 'byung ba ste/ 'dzam gling cshe la nges pa med/ rang rang dgos 'dod longs spyod ni/ 
6a4(kha): bsod nams las dbang bzhin du 'byung / skye ba gnas bzhi' mi rigs la/ 'dzam bu gling ni khyad par 'phags/ 'dzam bu gling gi mi la yang / mi gcig pa yi res drug ste/ dge 
6a5(kha): sdeg gnyis kyi snang ba la/ ye las yod khams dge ba 'byung / ngam las med khams sdeg pa 'byung / ye las 'byung ba'i rigs bzhi ste/ gtsug sgos dmu dang bya yi rigs/ rigs 
6a6(kha): bnod la tsril bani/ gzug n bya raba thag sdo' dba'/ k zhord pa tsab khyi brgya/ dsman gnun brgyu 'dan pa'i mtshag byan kun byi rgyug hra/ dbshan 
6b1(kha): la yang rigs lnga ste/ rgyal rigs dang ni rdje rigs dang / bram ze'i rigs dang dmangs rigs dang / gdol pa'i rigs dang lnga ru 'byung / de lnga la yang lnga lnga ste/ rigs ni nyi shu rtsa lnga'o// 
6b2(kha): rigs lnga de yi nang nas kyang / gnhen rab stong dang rtsa gnyis ni/ rgyal po'i rigs su skye ba bzhes/ bskal pa chen po ma s+dzogs bar/ rim gyis 'byon nas 'gro don mdzad/ 
6b3(kha): ghen rab re re 'byon dus su / gtsug skos dmu gsum dag gis ni/ lha gzhen srid pa gsum gsum 'byung / tshad med bzhi dang ye shes lnga/ 'gro ba sems can thams cad ni/ 
6b4(kha): thugs rjes thar par rab 'drin no// gnhen rab stong dang rtsa gnyis ni/ ye shes lnga yi bthu bskyed cing / srid pa bka' yi rgyud gnang nas/ gnhen gyis 'gro ba'i 'drin ston mdzad/ 
6b5(kha): slob dpon gshen rab bdag nyid ni/ da lha s+dzogs sku'i zhing khams 'dir/ ye shes ye khyab sgron ma la/ shes rab bskyed cing blo rtsal sbyang / srid pa stong rtsis gtan la phabs/ dus 
6b6(kha): 'dir bdag gi mtshan la ni/ mkhyen rtse rab mchog rgyal po'o// yab ni 'd khyab kun mkhyen rgyal/ yum ni yongs su gsal gdan ma/ bskal pa dbu ma'i dus nyid du // 
7a1(kha): sting gsum lye rud 'jig ten gyi/ rang 'byua khyen ldan gnas nyid du/ 'dren pa'i rten par dung 'dir byin/ gzen rab mu tsho sdam drug khyid/ bdag gis zhes rab'i/ 
7a2(kha): rtsal sbyang / stong dang rtsa gnyis ma s+dzogs bar/ sred pa rgyud kyi bon skos mdzod/ gzhen rab chen pos de gsungs nas/ 'gro ba'i don la thugs dgongs pa/ stong gsum khams / 
7a3(kha): gsum res drug ni/ thugs rjes thar par 'dren par 'gyur/ dpag med kun tu rab s+dzogs kyang / bskal pa dbu ma'i dus nyid la/ gshen rab stong dang rtsa gnyis ni/ rim gyis skye ba 
7a4(kha): bzhes pa ste/ stong dang rtsa gnyis sna 'dren pas/ ghen rab ghen rab chen po ste/ tshe lo ma tshe 'brum thub dus/ 'dren pa'i ston pa 'byen pa ni/ 'brum khri grlog gi tlhe can 
7a5(kha): byi/ skye ba'i yul ni kun shes bde ldan ma/ g.sung drung 'd khar mchod nyan mdun dung du/ rang 'byung mchod rten stong dang rtsa gnyis rtsar/ yab ni ye 'byung khri 'di la/ yum ni 
7a6(kha): kun shes bde ldan ma/ lha ni ye gsal mu med la/ srid pa yi sangs khyab pa'o// dpyad mkhan shes rab rab myur ro// mi tsho'i tshad ni 'bum phrag la/ gnhen rab sku tshe'i tshad / 
7b1(kha): ni 'bum phrag gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa'i bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ 'bum gyi phrag ni dgu yi bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs 
7b2(kha): gsung rab thams cad kyang / mkha' la rang bzhin 'od du yal/ ri yai rgyal po re rab kyang / ngo bo nyid kyi dbyings su gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten thams cad kyang / bdal pa chen po'i 
7b3(kha): dbyings su mnyam/ gshen rab khri kzhug ston pa yi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen 'd 'bar gnas/ lhun brtsegs gss mkhar mchod rten mdun drung du / yab ni thabs chen yi 
7b4(kha): mkhyen la/ yum ni shes rab kun snyoms par/ lha ni 'di dkar gnas 'dzin la/ srid pa phya rje ring khug go/ dpyad mkhan tshogs med ye mkhyen no// mi tsho'i tshad ni khri phrag 
7b5(kha): la/ gnhen rab sku tho'i tshad ni khri phrag gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khri phrag dgu yi bar du rab gnas shing / sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs 
7b6(kha): nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab gzha' res bzhin du yal/ re rab mkhan chen dbyings kyi ngo bo gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten con nyid klong du mnyam/ gnhen rab dag pa gti rgyal / 
8a1(kha): ye mkhyen kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni dhun sum 'tshigs pa'i gnas/ lo par shel gyi mchod ryten mdun dang du/ sab ni khri chen bar sa la/ sum zhi 'di btsun cang 
8a2(kha): mo'o// lha ni ye lha sgron ma la/ srid pa ba rgyung dkar po'o// dpyad mkhan shes rig don mkhas so// mi tsho' tshad ni steng phrag la/ gnhen rab sku tsho' tshad ni stong phrag gsum/ 
8a3(kha): 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ stong phrag dgu yi bar du gnas shing dar/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab rang bzhin 'od du yal/ 
8a4(kha): re rab mkhan chen dbyings kyi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten stong nyid ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab shes pa gsung snyan sgam po yi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'ol mo lung ring gnas/ zo bo / 
8a5(kha): khyung lag mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni rgyal bon thaMd dkar la/ yum ni yo phye rgyal bzhed ma/ lha ni gnen lha 'di dkar la/ srid pa sangs po 'bum khro'// dpyad mkhan 
8a6(kha): kun khyab kun shes so// mi tsho'i tsad ni brgya phrag la/ gshen rab sku tsho'i tshad ni brgya phrag gsum/ 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dgu yi bar du / 
8b1(kha): rab gnas kyang / sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab bya 'bur bzhin du yal/ re rab bye ba brgya phrag ngo bo gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten bde / 
8b2(kha): chen dbyings su mnyam/ gshen rab gsal ba tsig ma 'od rgyal gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni sku mkhar rab brten gnas/ g.yung drung 'khor lo mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni rgyal 
8b3(kha): bon thaMd dkar 'd dpag la/ yum ni bya btsun mu zer bang po gsal/ lha ni 'di lha gsal 'bar la/ srid pa gong sangs klong bdal lo// dpyad mkhan gsal shes kun mkhyen 
8b4(kha): no// mi tsho' tshad ni bcu phrag la/ ghen rab sku tsho' tshad ni bcu phrag gsum/ rab 'byams 'pul ngag con sde' bka' rgyud ni/ bye ba dgu yi bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung 
8b5(kha): thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab du phyis bzhin du yal/ re rab nga nyid don gyi ngo bo gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten bdal nyid dbyings su mnyam/ gzhan 
8b6(kha): rab 'di chen nyi ma'i rab gsal gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni kun 'byung tshogs pa'i gnas/ bkod pa rab mdzes mchod rten mdun drung du / yab ni kun ston 'di nyid rgyal ba dang / 
9a1(kha): sum zhi dpyad ma 'di nyid kun mdzes ma/ lha ni gklong chen bdal pa la/ srid pa bka' rgyud khrol nyid // dpyad mkhan shes rig tsigs med do// mi tsho'i chad ni bye ba / 
9a2(kha): la/ gnhen rab sku tsho'i tshad ni bye ba gsum/ 'dul gyi bana ngag con sde' bka' rgyud ni/ bye ba phrag ni dgu yi bar du gnas/ sku gsun thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ 
9a3(kha): sku gzugs gsung rab mkha' la 'od du yal/ re rab mkha' nyid don gyi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten mnyam nyid dbyings su mnyam/ ghen rab nyon mongs sdug bsngal 
9a4(kha): 'djoms byed kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rin chen 'od 'phro' gnas/ dung gi khri 'pangs mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni khri rgad 'di nyid rgyal po ste/ yum ni klong bdal byed ma 'od 
9a5(kha): btsun no/ lha n mkha' chen 'di bdal la/ sred pa ye gnasngs 'byungno// dpyad mkhan don la nges zhes so// m tsho' tshad ni sa ya la/ ghen rab sku tsho' tshad ns ya 
9a6(kha): gsum/ 'dul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ sa ya dgu yi bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab dngos med 'od du 
9b1(kha): yal/ re rab con nyid sems nyid ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten mkha' dbyings pa du mnyam/ gnhen rab thabs mkhas ye gsal rgyal po yi/ skye ba'i yul ni snang ldan / 
9b2(kha): lhun grub gnas/ mun 'dzoms 'di chen mchod nyen mdun dung du/ yab zhi thabs mkhas 'di steng rgyal/ yum ni kun ma bde btsun ni// lha ni snang sred ye mkhyen la/ srid 
9b3(kha): pa byams mgon dpag med do// dpyad mkhan ye shes ye 'byung ngo // mi tsho'i tshad ni 'brum phrag la/ gnhen rab sku tsho' tshad ni 'bum phrag gsum/ 'hrul ngag bden pa bon 
9b4(kha): sde' bka' rgyud ni/ 'brum prag dgu ya bar du gnas pa ste/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab snang dbyings nga du yal/ re rab mnyam snyoms 
9b5(kha): chen po ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten nam mkha' stong par mnyam/ gnhen rab ngng nyid klong bdal sgron ma yi/ skye ba'i yul ni rgyan ldan bskhod pa'i gnas/ rgyan bkod 
9b6(kha): khri skos mchod ryen mdun dung du / yab ni don dkar 'odi gsal dang / yum ni byams bskyed thang ma 'od/ lha ni kun dgongs mu med la/ srid pa dbyings nyid klong bdal lo// dpyad 
10a1(kha): mkhan reg rtsal nor med do// mi tshe'i tshad ni khri phrag la/ gshein rab sku tsho' tshad ni khre phrag gsum/ 'drul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khri phrag / 
10a2(kha): dgu .ye bar du gnas pa'i// sku gsu thugs kyi 'gro don dab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab na bun bzhin du yal/ re rab yongs khyab stobs chen ngo bor gcig/ sku gang 
10a3(kha): mchod rten ng bdal dbyings su mnyam/ gnhen rab thugs rje zhi dal a tshul gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'dod pa kun 'byung gnas/ dpe byad rgyan bzang mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab 
10a4(kha): ni byams snyoms sbyin 'gyed la/ yum ni kun snyoms 'di bdal lo// lha ni yongs khyab sgron ma la/ sred pa mkha' dbyings rgyud 'dzin no// dpyad mkhan tshogs med thabs ldan 
10a5(kha): no// mi tsho' tshad ni stong phrag la/ gnhen rab sku tsho' tshad ni stong phrag gsum/ 'hul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ stong phrag dgu yi bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung 
10a6(kha): thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab rang bzhin ngag du yal/ re rab tshad med byams snyoms ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten dbyings nyid pa du mnyam/ 
10b1(kha): gshen rab mi g.yo ye mkhyen rgyal ba yi/ skye ba'i yul ni gnas mcshog rgyan ldan gnas/ lhun 'thug brjid ldan mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni skyes mkhas rgyal po 
10b2(kha): la/ yum ni snying rje ldan mdzes ma/ lha ni thugs rjes lam 'dren la/ srid pa mi 'gyur kun mkhyen ni// dpyad mkhan rtsal rig myur ba'o// mi tsho' tshad ni brgya phrag la/ 
10b3(kha): gnhein rab sku tsho' tshad ni brgya phrag gsum/ 'dul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dgu yi bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ 
10b4(kha): / sku gzugs gsung rab skye med nga du yal/ re rab bdag med ngo bo nyid du gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten rang bzhin nga du mnyam/ gnhen rab a gtsug rgyal bdon ston gyi/ skye ba'i 
10b5(kha): yul ni mi 'gyur brtan pa'i gnas/ lo panga lhun brjid mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni yang rgyal khri 'di la/ yum ni lha mdzes 'di btsun ma/ lha ni dri med 'od gsal 
10b6(kha): la/ srid pa phyag gsal ye 'phrul lo// dpyad mkhan bde sgmra rang bzhin nga ston no// mi tsho'i tshad ni bcu phrag la/ gshen rab sku tsho' tshad ni bcu phrag gsum/ 'hrul ngag 
11a1(kha): bden pa tson sde' bka' rgyu ni/ bca srag dgu ya bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsu thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ skru gzugs gsu rab gna' tsim bzhin du 
11a2(kha): ysal/ de rab mthar thugs nyid kyi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten pa dang ngo bor mnyam/ gzhen rab gsal ba mun pas blib med kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni gna' tshen 'di 'bar 
11a3(kha): gnas/ gsar sdong po mchod rten mdun dung du/ yab ni dmangs gtsug rgyal 'di 'bar/ yum ni bde ldan 'odi thang gtsug/ lha ni ngag nyid bde ba la/ sred pa snang srid gs mdzad do// 
11a4(kha): dpyad mkhan rig pa thabs kyi brda ston no// mi tsho' tshad ni gcig gi phrag csu'o// gnhen rab sku tsho' tshad ni gcig phrag sum cu'o// 'dul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' 
11a5(kha): rgyud ni/ gcig gi srag ni dgu bcu' bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab dngos med mkha' la yal/ re rab dbyings s+dzogs chen 
11a6(kha): po'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten ci yang med par mnyam/ gnhen rab dbyings dag ye gsal rgyud ston gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni chad chen tshal gyi bling / dgur dgu khyud 
11b1(kha): mchod rnyen mdun dung du / yab ni gsal dag sung 'odi la/ yum ni sman sbyin gsos gyur ma/ lha ni yi gsal rgyud 'dzin la/ srid pa dpag med cis mkhyen no// dpyad mkhan 
11b2(kha): m nor thabs mkhas so// mi tsho' tshad ni bcu phrag bcu/ gnhen rab sku cshe bcu phrag sum tsu'o/ 'prul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ bcu ye phrag ni dgu bcu' 
11b3(kha): bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab hrig rgyu bzhin du yal/ re rab dmigs pa med pa'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten stong 
11b4(kha): gsal ngang du mnyam/ gshen rab ngang nyid gsal ldan shes rab kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni byin ldan bkod pa'i gnas/ rgyan bkod rab mdzes mchod rten mdun drung du / yab ni khri 
11b5(kha): nam 'd bdal la/ sum zhi 'di btsun yo bdal ma/ lha ni gtsug gsal ye gsal la/ sred pa 'byung ba'i skos 'debs 'o// dpyad mkchan thabs drug kun shes so// m tsho' 
11b6(kha): tshad ni brgya phrag bcug/ gshen rab sku che brgya phrag sum cu'o// 'hrul ngag bden pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ brgya phrag dgu bcu'i bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung thugs kyi 
12a1(kha): 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsun rab con byings pa du yal/ re rab don dam nyid kyi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mtshod nten byab chen dbyings su mnyam/ 
12a2(kha): gzhen rab dpag med don mdzad kun snyoms kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni gzha' tchen 'di 'khrigs gnas/ bkod ldan 'di 'khugs mchod rnyen mdun dung du/ yab ni kling 'bar gsal 
12a3(kha): mdog la/ yum ni bya btsun zer 'phro ma/ lha ni nga chen sgrib med la/ srid pa mkha' gsang kling 'phyo'o// dpyad mkhan rig shes rmad gyur ro// mi tsho' tshad ni steng phrag bcu / 
12a4(kha): gshen rab sku che stong phrag sum hu'o// 'prul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ stong gi phrag ni dgu bcu' bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku / 
12a5(kha): gzugs gsung rab 'di yal bzhin du yal/ re rab sproes bral bde chen ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten dag chen nga du mnyam/ gnhen rab byams mgon yi gtsug rgyal 
12a6(kha): ba yi/ skye ba'i yul ni seang gi rgyab bsgol gnas/ zo b rtse dgu mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni rgyal po byams gtsug rgyal/ yum ni yongs bskyed bdag nyid ma/ lha ni 
12b1(kha): ye shes dgongs chen la/ srid pa 'byung ba'i dbang sgyur ro// dpyad mkhan don mgyur rig 'byed do// mi tsho' tshad ni khri phrag bcug/ gshen rab sku che khri phrag sum cu'o// 'phrul ngag 
12b2(kha): bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khre phrag dgu bcla' bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsun thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab rang bzhin med par yal/ re rab 
12b3(kha): bon nyid stong pa'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten rtsol bral ngng du mnyam/ ghen rab ting gtsug 'di 'phro rab gsal gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni sman mchog tshal gyi gnas// 
12b4(kha): g.yung drung bkod legs mchod rnten mdun drung du/ yab ni rgyal po 'di ston la/ yum ni sbyin gtong kun tshims ma/ lha ni ting 'dzin rgyud nyid la/ srid pa spyad ldan skos 'debs

12b6(kha): dgu bcu' bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab me tog 'od du yal/ re rab ye nas ngo bor nyid du gcig/ sku gdung mchod / 
13a1(kha): / #/ rten yi khyab dbyings su mnyam/ gshen rab byad ldan dag pa'i 'di nyid kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni bkod ldan mdzes pa'i gnas/ hri skos rgyal ba mchod rtyen mdun dung du // 
13a2(kha): yab zhi kun gzigs rgyal ba la/ yum ni kun la dbyings khyab ma/ lha ni ghen rab rgyud 'dren la/ sried pa 'byung ba'i rgyu bskyed do// dpyad mkhan myur ba tshad shes so// ma / 
13a3(kha): tsho'i tshad ni sa ya bcung / ghen rab sku tchegs ya sum tu'o// 'bhrul ngag ldan pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ sa ya dgu bcu' bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don 
13a4(kha): rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab snang gsal 'od du yal/ re rab mkha' klong dbyings kyi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten klong dbyings pa du mnyam/ gshen rab nyi ma'i 'od 
13a5(kha): nyid zer 'phros/ skye ba'i yul nhi bdal snyoms dag pa'i gnas/ 'de gdugs rgyal mtshan mchod nyen mbdun du du/ sabzhi don gsal rgyal bala/ sum n kun bal long 
13a6(kha): nyid ma/ lha ni gting dag sangs ldan la/ srid pa mu med gting ring ngo // dpyad mkhan kun gsal don gyur ro// mi tsho' tshad ni bye ba bcu / ghen rab sku tsho bye ba sum cu'o// 
13b1(kha): 'bhrul ngag ldan pa bon sde'i bka' rgyud ni/ bye ba phrag ni dgu yi bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab snang med ngang du yal/ re rab / 
13b2(kha): ma bcos pa yi ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten khyab bdal dbyings su mnyam/ gnhen rab ye gsal snang med 'di khyab kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni ren chen bkod tshal gnas/ 
13b3(kha): bsam legs rgyan bzang mchod rten mdun drung du/ yab ni dbang chen kun sgyur rgyal/ yum ni brten nyid 'di btsun tang / lha ni ye 'byung mu med la/ srid pa pbya rje ye 'dhrul 
13b4(kha): lo// dpyad mkhan don rtogs rab mkhas so// mi tsho' tshad ni dug pbyur bcu / gzhin rab sku che dung phyur sum su'o// 'phrul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ dung spyur phrag ni 
13b5(kha): dgu bcu' bar du gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab rang bzhin med par yal/ re rab dag pa med pa'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod 
13b6(kha): rten mkha' khyab bdal par mnyam/ gshen rab 'khor ba bde bar rab 'drin gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni 'di mdzes dper bkod gnas/ byin chen dpag pa mchod rnyen mdun drung du / 
14a1(kha): yab ni don 'dzin 'di gting rgyal/ yum ni 'di skying bhang mo btsun/ lha ni don dgongs 'di gsal la/ srid pa 'phrul gyi gting rnam mo// dpyad mkhan thabs drug 
14a2(kha): kun ston no// mi tsho' tshad ni khrag khrig bcug/ gnhen rab sku tshe khrag khrig sum su'o// 'brul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig phrag ni dgu bcu' bar du 
14a3(kha): gnas/ sku gsung thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab gu zlo' 'od du yal/ re rab dpag med bdal pa'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten rab 'byams

14a5(kha): gsal rgyal po dang / yum ni kun bskyed rab 'od ma/ lha ni kun khyab nam mkha' la/ srid pa mkha' yangs kun shes so// dpyad mkhan las rtsis thabs gsal lo// mi 
14a6(kha): tsho' tshad ni hrag khrig brgya/ gshen rab sku ce khrag khrig sum brgya'o/ 'pbrul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khrag hrig dgu brgya' bar du rab tu gnas/ sku gsung 
14b1(kha): thuags kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab 'di snang dbyings su yal/ re rab ye bdal chen po'i ngo bor gcig/ sku gdung mchod rten mkha' dbyings stong par mnyam/ 
14b2(kha): gnhen rab chags med pbyin pa yongs snyims kyi/ skye ba'i yul ni rab bskod dag pa'i gnas/ rin chen 'di 'bar mchod nyen mdun dung du/ yab ni rgyal po gzi byen 'bar/

14b6(kha): gyi/ skye ba'i yul ni dgos 'dod kun 'byung gnas/ dpag med 'di snang mchod rten mdun drung du / yab zni gsal ba don nyid rgyal/ yum ni chags med kun snyoms ma/ lha ni 
15a1(kha): 'd gsal don 'bar ma/ sred pa bya ye shes drug go/ dpyad mtkhan tchad ston bo gyur ro// mtsho' shad ni khrag brig tri/ gzen rab sku me brag brig dum khro'o// 
15a2(kha): 'dul ngag bden pa bon sde' bka' rgyud ni/ khrag khrig dgu khri' bar du gnas pa'o// sku gsu thugs kyi 'gro don rab s+dzogs nas/ sku gzugs gsung rab dngos med pga du yal/
